### [176] [Finite Blocklength Covert Communication over Quasi-Static Multiple-Antenna Fading Channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29645)
*Changhong Liu,Jingjing Wang,Qiaosheng Zhang,Jinpeng Xu,Lin Zhou*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 该论文研究了准静态多天线衰落信道下隐蔽通信的有限码长性能，证明了隐蔽速率满足平方根定律，多天线系统能提供显著的空间分集增益，且合法用户的信道状态信息可用性不影响隐蔽通信性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 国际电信联盟白皮书呼吁在衰落信道上实现极高安全性和低延迟通信。低延迟要求对应准静态衰落模型，而高安全性可通过隐蔽通信实现。为响应ITU的号召，研究准静态多天线衰落信道下隐蔽通信的有限码长性能。

Method: 使用Kullback-Leibler散度作为隐蔽性度量，研究合法发射机和接收机信道状态信息可用性的所有四种情况，假设看守者知道从合法发射机到自身的完美信道状态信息。将准η邻域框架扩展到衰落信道，并处理随机信道矩阵带来的挑战。对于可靠性分析，由于隐蔽性约束导致的功率衰减，通过仔细控制高阶项并利用隐蔽中断概率特性，改进了Yang等人的非隐蔽分析。

Result: 当码长为n时，一阶隐蔽速率满足平方根定律，以Θ(n^{-1/2})缩放，系数由合法用户和看守者信道矩阵的迹决定，二阶速率消失。与Yang等人的非隐蔽结果不同，合法用户的信道状态信息可用性不影响隐蔽通信的有限码长性能。多天线系统为隐蔽通信提供了显著的空间分集增益。

Conclusion: 在准静态多天线衰落信道下，隐蔽通信的有限码长性能遵循平方根定律，多天线系统能提供重要的空间分集优势，且信道状态信息对隐蔽通信性能的影响与非隐蔽情况不同，合法用户的信道状态信息可用性不影响隐蔽通信性能。

Abstract: The white book released by the International Telecommunications Union (ITU) calls for extremely high-security and low-latency communication over fading channels. Under the low-latency requirement, the corresponding fading model is quasi-static fading while high-security can be achieved via covert communication. In response to the call of ITU, we study the finite blocklength performance of optimal codes for covert communication over quasi-static multi-antenna fading channels, under the covertness metric of Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence. In particular, we study all four cases regarding the availability of channel state information (CSI) for legitimate transmitter and receiver, and assume that the warden knows perfect CSI for the channel from the legitimate transmitter to itself. Specifically, we show that, when the blocklength is $n$, the first-order covert rate satisfies the square root law, scaling as $Θ(n^{-\frac{1}{2}})$ with the coefficient determined by the traces of the channel matrices of the legitimate users and the warden, and the second-order rate vanishes. In contrast to the non-covert result of Yang et al. (TIT, 2014), we show that CSI availability at the legitimate users does not affect the finite blocklength performance for covert communication. Furthermore, we reveal the significant spatial diversity gain provided by multiple-antenna systems for covert communication. For the covertness analysis, we extend the quasi-$η$-neighborhood framework to fading channels and address challenges arising from the random channel matrices. For the reliability analysis, due to the vanishing power imposed by the covertness constraint, we refine the non-covert analysis by Yang et al. (TIT, 2014), by carefully controlling higher-order terms and exploiting the properties of covert outage probability.

</details>


### [177] [Joint Identification and Sensing with Noisy Feedback: A Task-Oriented Communication Framework for 6G](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29649)
*Yaning Zhao,Holger Boche,Christian Deppe*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究带噪声严格因果反馈的状态相关离散无记忆信道上的联合识别与感知(JIDAS)，推导了容量-失真函数的下界和上界，量化了噪声反馈下JIDAS的基本极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 面向任务的通信是6G系统的关键使能技术，其目标是支持决策和行动而非完整消息重建。从信息论角度看，识别(ID)码为此范式提供了自然抽象，使接收器能够测试是否发送了任务相关消息，而无需解码整个消息。受反馈对ID的强烈影响以及通信感知一体化日益增长的兴趣驱动，本文研究带噪声严格因果反馈的状态相关离散无记忆信道上的联合识别与感知。

Method: 研究带噪声严格因果反馈的状态相关离散无记忆信道上的联合识别与感知(JIDAS)。对于确定性和随机化编码方案，推导了容量-失真函数的下界和上界。通过反馈信号，发射机在传输识别消息的同时估计信道状态。

Result: 推导了JIDAS在噪声反馈下的容量-失真函数的下界和上界，量化了JIDAS的基本极限。结果将现有的无噪声反馈特性恢复为特例，表明噪声反馈下的性能界限。

Conclusion: 本文为带噪声反馈的联合识别与感知提供了理论基础，量化了其基本性能极限。研究结果将现有的无噪声反馈特性作为特例包含在内，为6G系统中面向任务的通信设计提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Task-oriented communication is a key enabler of emerging 6G systems, where the objective is to support decisions and actions rather than full message reconstruction. From an information-theoretic perspective, identification (ID) codes provide a natural abstraction for this paradigm by enabling receivers to test whether a task-relevant message was sent, without decoding the entire message. Motivated by the strong impact of feedback on ID and by the growing interest in integrated communication and sensing, this paper studies joint identification and sensing (JIDAS) over state-dependent discrete memoryless channels with noisy strictly causal feedback. The transmitter conveys identification messages while simultaneously estimating the channel state from the feedback signal. For both deterministic and randomized coding schemes, we derive lower and upper bounds on the capacity--distortion function. The results quantify the fundamental limits of JIDAS under noisy feedback and recover existing noiseless-feedback characterizations as special cases.

### [178] [α-Fair Multistatic ISAC Beamforming for Multi-User MIMO-OFDM Systems via Riemannian Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29717)
*Hyeonho Noh,Jonggyu Jang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出了一种α-公平的多基地集成感知与通信框架，用于多用户MIMO-OFDM系统，通过优化每个目标的CRLB来实现感知公平性


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作通常优化聚合感知指标，这会偏向几何位置有利的目标，导致感知不公平。需要一种能够确保所有目标公平感知性能的方法

Method: 采用α-公平效用函数最小化每个目标的CRLB，在满足用户最小数据速率和发射功率约束下，通过黎曼共轭梯度方法和光滑惩罚重构解决非凸优化问题

Result: 仿真结果验证了所提方案在实现有利的感知公平性与通信性能权衡方面的有效性

Conclusion: 提出的α-公平多基地ISAC框架能够有效解决感知不公平问题，在保证通信性能的同时实现所有目标的公平感知

Abstract: This paper proposes an $α$-fair multistatic integrated sensing and communication (ISAC) framework for multi-user multi-input multi-output (MIMO)-orthogonal frequency division multiplexing (OFDM) systems, where communication users act as passive bistatic receivers to enable multistatic sensing. Unlike existing works that optimize aggregate sensing metrics and thus favor geometrically advantageous targets, we minimize the $α$-fairness utility over per-target Cramér--Rao lower bounds (CRLBs) subject to per-user minimum data rate and transmit power constraints. The resulting non-convex problem is solved via the Riemannian conjugate gradient (RCG) method with a smooth penalty reformulation. Simulation results validate the effectiveness of the proposed scheme in achieving a favorable sensing fairness--communication trade-off.

</details>


### [179] [Implementing Basic Arithmetic in $\mathbb{F}_p$ via $\mathbb{F}_2$, and Its Application for Computing the Hamming Distance of Linear Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29942)
*Fernando Hernando,Gregorio Quintana-Ortí*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 提出一种在任意素数域F_p上进行基本算术运算的新方法，使用F_2上的传统二进制运算，该方法高效且具有竞争力，应用于计算随机线性码的最小汉明距离


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 需要一种在有限域F_p上进行高效算术运算的方法，特别是为了计算随机线性码的最小汉明距离，现有方法在性能上存在改进空间

Method: 使用F_2上的传统二进制运算来实现F_p上的基本算术运算，采用等距加法等新技术加速汉明距离计算，开发了C语言实现

Result: 新方法在单核处理器、多核处理器和共享内存多处理器上明显优于Magma和GAP/Guava等现有软件，在F_3和F_7域上的汉明距离计算中表现出色

Conclusion: 提出的基于F_2二进制运算的F_p算术方法高效且具有竞争力，特别适用于计算随机线性码的最小汉明距离，在实际应用中显著提升了计算性能

Abstract: We present a new general method for performing basic arithmetic in the finite field~$\mathbb{F}_p$ for any prime $p>2$ by using traditional binary operations over~$\mathbb{F}_2$. Our new approach is efficient and competitive with current state-of-art methods. We apply our new arithmetic method to the computation of the minimum Hamming distance of random linear codes for the fields $\mathbb{F}_3$ and $\mathbb{F}_7$. Our new arithmetic method allows to apply new techniques such as the isometric addition that accelerate the computation of the Hamming distance. We have developed implementations in the C programming language for computing the Hamming distance that clearly outperform both state-of-art licensed software and open-source software such as \textsc{Magma} and \textsc{GAP}/\textsc{Guava} on single-core processors, multicore processors, and shared-memory multiprocessors.

</details>


### [180] [Reducing Subpacketization in Device-to-Device Coded Caching via Heterogeneous File Splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.29945)
*Xiang Zhang,Giuseppe Caire,Mingyue Ji*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文扩展了基于包类型的D2D编码缓存框架，从同质包大小扩展到异质包大小，通过联合优化包大小、用户分组和多播发射器选择来最小化峰值回程负载，同时保持最优通信速率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于包类型的D2D编码缓存方案只考虑同质包大小（所有包类型大小相同），这限制了在某些参数范围内峰值回程负载的进一步降低。需要扩展框架以支持异质包大小来获得更好的性能。

Method: 扩展包类型框架到异质包大小，允许不同包类型具有不同大小。联合优化包大小、用户分组和多播发射器选择，在保持最优速率的同时最小化峰值回程负载。针对特定参数(K, KM/N)=(2q+1, 2r)构造新的D2D编码缓存方案。

Result: 提出的异质包类型构造在特定参数范围内实现了相对于Ji-Caire-Molisch方案的常数因子峰值回程负载降低，并补充了现有包类型设计不适用的参数范围。

Conclusion: 异质包大小扩展了包类型框架的能力，在保持最优通信速率的同时实现了更好的峰值回程负载性能，为D2D编码缓存提供了更灵活的设计空间。

Abstract: The packet type (PT)-based framework~\cite{zhang2026taming} provides a systematic and principled approach to designing device-to-device (D2D) coded caching schemes that achieve reduced \sbp while preserving the optimal communication rate. However, existing PT designs rely exclusively on homogeneous \sbp, where all packets have an identical size regardless of their types. This restriction limits the achievable \sbp reduction in certain parameter regimes. In this paper, we extend the PT framework to \emph{heterogeneous} \sbp, allowing packet sizes to vary across types under a refined type classification. The packet sizes, in conjunction with user grouping and multicast transmitter selection, are jointly optimized to minimize the overall \sbp level while preserving the optimal rate. Based on the heterogeneous PT framework, we construct a new class of D2D coded caching schemes for $(K, KM/N)=(2q+1, 2r)$ with $q,r \in \mathbb{N}_+$, where $K,N$ and $M$ denote the number of users, files and cache memory size, respectively. The proposed construction achieves a constant-factor reduction in \sbp compared to the Ji-Caire-Molisch (JCM) caching scheme~\cite{ji2016fundamental} and complements existing PT designs that are not applicable in this parameter regime.

</details>
